‚úÖ Your phone number will not be shared with the campaign, or anyone on our server. Only Discord will have this information. For more on this, please see [Discord's Privacy Policy](https://discord.com/privacy).

üõë If your phone number is not verified by **Sept. 16th**, you will not be able to send messages or interact in the server until verified.

Go to your devise and enter this link into Google: https://events.democrats.org/event/672393/ 

Scroll down to the section that says sign up and fill in your information, then click the date and time that works best for you. You should then receive a message by text saying your confirmed for training.

As for a scroll issue, if you are on a mobile devise scroll down by swiping up with your finger, if on PC with mouse use the roller on the mouse and scroll down. If on laptop place two fingers on the pad and swipe up with them. I hope this answered you question.
--------------------
